  my <span class=GramE>childhood ,I</span> always thought my dream was to be a Software
  Engineer. It seemed like an appropriate path and my interest towards
  computers and coding increased <span class=SpellE>tremendiously</span>. It
  even gravitated me towards doing many Internships and contributed code for
